SECTION      II.

Of  the  Origin  of  Ideas.

*

XLVERY  one  will  readily  allow  that  there  is  a

thought  is  ftill  inferior  to  the  duUeft  fenfation.

juft    conception    of  his  fituationj    but  never  can

miftake  that  conception  for  the  real  difordcrs
